on controller{thread-unsafe}
	ignore_controller{Builtin, None}
	declare local controller_value[MAX::CB::STACK{int}] : int[] {Reuses: 0}
	controller_value[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} := CC[CC_NUM{int}]{int}
	if(CC_NUM{int} = 1)
				frame1{int} := CC[1]{int}
				call buffer_modwheel_animation{UserDefined, Call}


		set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_modwheel_slider{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, CC[1]{int}){Builtin, None}
	end if
	if(CC_NUM{int} = 64)
		if(CC[64]{int} > 63)
			sustain_pedal_actual{int} := ON{int}
		else
			sustain_pedal_actual{int} := OFF{int}
			sustain_pedal{int} := OFF{int}
			i{int} := 0
			while(i{int} <= 127) 
				if(pressed_keys[i{int}]{int} = - 1)
					ii{int} := 0
					while(ii{int} <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} - 1)) 
							declare local ks1 : int {Reuses: 0}
							declare local i9 : int {Reuses: 0}
							declare local release_offset0 : int {Reuses: 0}
							declare local _ret220 : int {Reuses: 0}
							declare local result20 : int {Reuses: 1}
							declare local result21 : int {Reuses: 1}
							declare local is_active00 : int {Reuses: 3}
							declare local i60 : int {Reuses: 1}
							declare local i501 : int {Reuses: 2}
							declare local result22 : int {Reuses: 1}
							declare local result23 : int {Reuses: 1}
							declare local result30 : int {Reuses: 1}
							declare local result24 : int {Reuses: 1}
								instrument_slot1{int} := ii{int}
								note5{int} := i{int}
								ks1{int} := ks1{int}
								i9{int} := i9{int}
								release_offset0{int} := release_offset0{int}
								_ret220{int} := _ret220{int}
								result20{int} := result20{int}
								result21{int} := result21{int}
								is_active00{int} := is_active00{int}
								i60{int} := i60{int}
								i501{int} := i501{int}
								result22{int} := result22{int}
								result23{int} := result23{int}
								result30{int} := result30{int}
								result24{int} := result24{int}
								call articulations_note_off{UserDefined, Call}


						inc(ii{int}){Builtin, None}
					end while
				end if
				inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
		end if
	end if
			wait_time0{int} := (lookahead{int} * 1000) * use_constant_delay{int}
			call wait_or_zero{UserDefined, Call}


	sustain_pedal{int} := sustain_pedal_actual{int}
	if(CC_NUM{int} = 1)
				note13{int} := 0
				value5{int} := controller_value[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}

			update_keyswitch_volume_curve{UserDefined, Call}

	end if
end on

on ui_control(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){thread-unsafe}
	xy_modwheel_assignment[0 + 1]{real} := 1
	xy_modwheel_assignment[4 + 1]{real} := 1
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN{int})
		if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 0) or (get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 4))
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fade_circle_md{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	else
		if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_UP{int})
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fade_circle_md{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
	ma_cb_id{int} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}
	if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 2) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real}))
		if(xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} < xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real})
			xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} := xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real}
		end if
		loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int} := int(xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real} * 127){Builtin, None}
	else
		if(((get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 0) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real})) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real}))
			set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fade_circle_md{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None} - 20){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
			loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int} := int(round((xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} - xy_modwheel_assignment[2]{real}) * 127){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		else
			if(((get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 4) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real})) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real}))
				set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_fade_circle_md{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}, get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_X{int}){Builtin, None} + int(xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real} * real(get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_WIDTH{int}){Builtin, None} - 20){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
				loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int} := int((xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real} - xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real}) * 127){Builtin, None}
			else
				if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_modwheel_assignment{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 6) and (xy_modwheel_assignment[0]{real} <= xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real}))
					if(xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real} > xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real})
						xy_modwheel_assignment[4]{real} := xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real}
					end if
					loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int} := int(xy_modwheel_assignment[6]{real} * 127){Builtin, None}
				end if
			end if
		end if
	end if
	wait(10000){Builtin, None}
	if(ma_cb_id{int} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{int})
			update_modwheel_assignment_control{UserDefined, Call}

			update_modwheel_assignment_circles{UserDefined, Call}

	end if
end on

on ui_control(xy_dynamic_range{real[]}){thread-unsafe}
	dr_cb_id{int} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}
	if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_dynamic_range{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 0) and (xy_dynamic_range[0]{real} <= xy_dynamic_range[2]{real}))
		loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int} := int(xy_dynamic_range[0]{real} * 127){Builtin, None}
	else
		if((get_control_par(get_ui_id(xy_dynamic_range{real[]}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_ACTIVE_INDEX{int}){Builtin, None} = 2) and (xy_dynamic_range[0]{real} <= xy_dynamic_range[2]{real}))
			loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int} := int(xy_dynamic_range[2]{real} * 127){Builtin, None}
		end if
	end if
	wait(10000){Builtin, None}
	if(dr_cb_id{int} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{int})
			update_dynamic_range_control{UserDefined, Call}

	end if
end on

on ui_control(xy_center_circles{real[]}){thread-unsafe}
	cc_cb_id{int} := NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}
	declare local angle[MAX::CB::STACK{int}] : real[] {Reuses: 0}
	declare local value[MAX::CB::STACK{int}] : int[] {Reuses: 0}
	declare local distance[MAX::CB::STACK{int}] : real[] {Reuses: 0}
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN{int})
			declare local dx0 : real {Reuses: 0}
			declare local dy0 : real {Reuses: 0}
				ret15{real} := distance[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}
				x17{real} := xy_center_circles[0]{real}
				y3{real} := xy_center_circles[1]{real}
				dx0{real} := dx0{real}
				dy0{real} := dy0{real}
				center_circle_distance{UserDefined, Inlining}


			declare local dx1 : real {Reuses: 0}
			declare local dy1 : real {Reuses: 0}
			declare local cos_theta0 : real {Reuses: 0}
			declare local angle1 : real {Reuses: 0}
				ret16{real} := angle[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}
				x18{real} := xy_center_circles[0]{real}
				y4{real} := xy_center_circles[1]{real}
				dx1{real} := dx1{real}
				dy1{real} := dy1{real}
				cos_theta0{real} := cos_theta0{real}
				angle1{real} := angle1{real}
				center_circle_angle{UserDefined, Inlining}


			declare local new_angle0 : real {Reuses: 0}
				ret17{int} := value[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}
				angle0{real} := angle[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}
				angle_min0{real} := 0.7
				angle_max0{real} := (NI_MATH_PI{real} * 2) - 0.7
				new_angle0{real} := new_angle0{real}
				call angle_to_value{UserDefined, Call}


		if((distance[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} >= 0.32) and (distance[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} < 0.36))
			selected_subarticulation{int} := 0
		else
			if((distance[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} >= 0.36) and (distance[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} < 0.4))
				selected_subarticulation{int} := 1
			else
				if((distance[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} >= 0.4) and (distance[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} < 0.44))
					selected_subarticulation{int} := 2
				else
					if((distance[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} >= 0.44) and (distance[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real} < 0.48))
						selected_subarticulation{int} := 3
					end if
				end if
			end if
		end if
		if(abs(value[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} - loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} < 10)
			selected_circle_end{int} := 0
		else
			if(abs(value[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} - loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} < 10)
				selected_circle_end{int} := 1
			else
				selected_circle_end{int} := - 1
			end if
		end if
			declare local idx170 : int {Reuses: 0}
				idx170{int} := idx170{int}
				call update_subarticulation_selection{UserDefined, Call}


	end if
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DRAG{int})
		wait(10000){Builtin, None}
		if((cc_cb_id{int} = NI_CALLBACK_ID{int}) and (selected_circle_end{int} # - 1))
				declare local dx1 : real {Reuses: 0}
				declare local dy1 : real {Reuses: 0}
				declare local cos_theta0 : real {Reuses: 0}
				declare local angle1 : real {Reuses: 0}
					ret16{real} := angle[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}
					x18{real} := xy_center_circles[0]{real}
					y4{real} := xy_center_circles[1]{real}
					dx1{real} := dx1{real}
					dy1{real} := dy1{real}
					cos_theta0{real} := cos_theta0{real}
					angle1{real} := angle1{real}
					center_circle_angle{UserDefined, Inlining}


				declare local new_angle0 : real {Reuses: 0}
					ret17{int} := value[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}
					angle0{real} := angle[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{real}
					angle_min0{real} := 0.7
					angle_max0{real} := (NI_MATH_PI{real} * 2) - 0.7
					new_angle0{real} := new_angle0{real}
					call angle_to_value{UserDefined, Call}


			if(selected_circle_end{int} = 0)
				if(value[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} < ((loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int} - loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int}) - loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int}))
					loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int} := value[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}
				end if
			else
				if(selected_circle_end{int} = 1)
					if(value[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int} > ((loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int} + loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int}) + loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int}))
						loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int} := value[NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} mod MAX::CB::STACK{int}]{int}
					end if
				end if
			end if
				update_modwheel_assignment_control{UserDefined, Call}

				update_modwheel_assignment_circles{UserDefined, Call}

		end if
	end if
end on

on ui_control(btn_factory_reset{int})
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local ii : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local iii : int {Reuses: 0}
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} - 1)) 
		octave_layer[i{int}]{int} := 0
		octave_shift[i{int}]{int} := 0
		ii{int} := 0
		while(ii{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
			articulation_names[i{int}, ii{int}]{string} := "Empty"
			articulation_volume_min[i{int}, ii{int}]{int} := 0
			articulation_volume_max[i{int}, ii{int}]{int} := 127
			articulation_volume_curve[i{int}, ii{int}]{int} := 0
			articulation_humanization[i{int}, ii{int}]{int} := 0
			articulation_release[i{int}, ii{int}]{int} := - 1
			iii{int} := 0
			while(iii{int} <= (4 - 1)) 
				loaded_subarticulations[i{int}, ii{int}, iii{int}]{int} := - 1
				loaded_subarticulations_start[i{int}, ii{int}, iii{int}]{int} := 0
				loaded_subarticulations_end[i{int}, ii{int}, iii{int}]{int} := 127
				loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[i{int}, ii{int}, iii{int}]{int} := 0
				loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[i{int}, ii{int}, iii{int}]{int} := 0
				loaded_subarticulations_volume[i{int}, ii{int}, iii{int}]{int} := 0
				loaded_subarticulations_tightness[i{int}, ii{int}, iii{int}]{int} := 0
				loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[i{int}, ii{int}, iii{int}]{int} := 0
				loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[i{int}, ii{int}, iii{int}]{int} := 127
				loaded_subarticulations_vibrato[i{int}, ii{int}, iii{int}]{int} := 0
				loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[i{int}, ii{int}, iii{int}]{int} := 0

function update_purge{restricted}
	i17{int} := 0
	ii4{int} := 0
	iii1{int} := 0
	subarticulation_is_loaded0{int[]} := [0]
	i17{int} := 0
	while(i17{int} <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} - 1)) 
		ii4{int} := 0
		while(ii4{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
			iii1{int} := 0
			while(iii1{int} <= (4 - 1)) 
				if(loaded_subarticulations[i17{int}, ii4{int}, iii1{int}]{int} # - 1)
					subarticulation_is_loaded0[loaded_subarticulations[i17{int}, ii4{int}, iii1{int}]{int}]{int} := subarticulation_is_loaded0[loaded_subarticulations[i17{int}, ii4{int}, iii1{int}]{int}]{int} + keyswitch_purge_states[i17{int}, ii4{int}]{int}
				end if
				inc(iii1{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
			inc(ii4{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		inc(i17{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	i17{int} := 0
	while(i17{int} <= (NUM_SUBARTICULATIONS{int} - 1)) 
		if(subarticulations_group_idx[i17{int}]{int} # NI_NOT_FOUND{int})
			if(subarticulation_is_loaded0[i17{int}]{int} = 0)
						subarticulation_id1{int} := i17{int}
						purge_state0{int} := OFF{int}
						_ret660{int} := _ret6600{int}
						group_count00{int} := group_count000{int}
						subarticulation_purge{UserDefined, Inlining}


			end if
		end if
		inc(i17{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	i17{int} := 0
	while(i17{int} <= (NUM_SUBARTICULATIONS{int} - 1)) 
		if(subarticulations_group_idx[i17{int}]{int} # NI_NOT_FOUND{int})
			if(subarticulation_is_loaded0[i17{int}]{int} > 0)
						subarticulation_id1{int} := i17{int}
						purge_state0{int} := ON{int}
						_ret660{int} := group_count000{int}
						group_count00{int} := group_count001{int}
						subarticulation_purge{UserDefined, Inlining}


			end if
		end if
		inc(i17{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function sh_right_safe(val0 : int, pos0 : int)
	return ((sh_right(val0{int}, 31){Builtin, None} .and. (1 * sh_left(1, 31 - pos0{int}){Builtin, None})) .or. sh_right(val0{int} .and. 2147483647, pos0{int}){Builtin, None})
end function

function is_in_range(value0 : int, a0 : int, b0 : int)
	return (1 + (sh_right(b0{int} - value0{int}, 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(value0{int} - a0{int}, 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function swap(a1 : int, b1 : int)
	a1{int} := a1{int} .xor. b1{int}
	b1{int} := b1{int} .xor. a1{int}
	a1{int} := a1{int} .xor. b1{int}
end function

function gt(a2 : int, b2 : int)

function tinylist.print(ls13 : int)
	declare local bl : string := "[" {Reuses: 0}
	lib.i{int} := 0
	while(lib.i{int} <= ((31 / ((ls13{int} .and. 3) + 2)) - 1)) 
		bl{string} := bl{string} & tinylist.get(ls13{int}, lib.i{int}){UserDefined, None}
		if(lib.i{int} < ((31 / ((ls13{int} .and. 3) + 2)) - 1))
			bl{string} := bl{string} & ", "
		end if
		inc(lib.i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	bl{string} := bl{string} & "]"
	message(bl{string}){Builtin, None}
end function

		inc(tests.counter_successful{int}){Builtin, None}
		_test_message_successful(tests.counter_successful{int} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{int}, result{int}, expected0{unknown}, tests.time_elapsed{int}){UserDefined, None}
	else
		inc(tests.counter_unsuccessful{int}){Builtin, None}
		_test_message_unsuccessful(tests.counter_successful{int} + tests.counter_unsuccessful{int}, result{int}, expected0{unknown}, tests.time_elapsed{int}){UserDefined, None}
	end if
end function

end function

function assert_side_effects(func3 : unknown, variable0 : unknown, expected1 : unknown)

function last_transitions_add_event

	min3{int} := last_transitions_timecode[instrument2{int}, keyswitch1{int}, subarticulation_idx1{int}, 0]{int}
	min_idx0{int} := 0

	if(transition_type0{int} >= 0)
		i13{int} := 0
		while(i13{int} <= 7) 
			if(last_transitions[instrument2{int}, keyswitch1{int}, subarticulation_idx1{int}, i13{int}]{int} = - 1)
				idx24{int} := i13{int}
				if(min3{int} > last_transitions_timecode[instrument2{int}, keyswitch1{int}, subarticulation_idx1{int}, i13{int}]{int})

					min_idx0{int} := i13{int}
				end if
			end if
			inc(i13{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while

function articulations_compute_level
	subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} := 0
	fade_in_start0{int} := loaded_subarticulations_start[instrument_slot2{int}, keyswitch3{int}, subarticulation2{int}]{int}
	fade_in_range0{int} := loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[instrument_slot2{int}, keyswitch3{int}, subarticulation2{int}]{int}
	fade_out_end0{int} := loaded_subarticulations_end[instrument_slot2{int}, keyswitch3{int}, subarticulation2{int}]{int}
	fade_out_range0{int} := loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[instrument_slot2{int}, keyswitch3{int}, subarticulation2{int}]{int}
	if(in_range(get_modulation_position(note6{int}){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}, fade_in_start0{int}, fade_out_end0{int}){Builtin, None})
		subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} := 1
		if(in_range(get_modulation_position(note6{int}){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}, fade_in_start0{int}, fade_in_start0{int} + fade_in_range0{int}){Builtin, None} and (fade_in_range0{int} > 0))
			subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} := real(get_modulation_position(note6{int}){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} - fade_in_start0{int}){Builtin, None} / real(fade_in_range0{int}){Builtin, None}
		else
			if(in_range(get_modulation_position(note6{int}){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}, fade_out_end0{int} - fade_out_range0{int}, fade_out_end0{int}){Builtin, None} and (fade_out_range0{int} > 0))
				subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real} := real(fade_out_end0{int} - get_modulation_position(note6{int}){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}){Builtin, None} / real(fade_out_range0{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if
		end if
	end if
	ret9{int} := int(1e+06 * ((real(articulations_compute_volume_curve(articulation_volume_min[instrument_slot2{int}, keyswitch3{int}]{int}, articulation_volume_max[instrument_slot2{int}, keyswitch3{int}]{int}, real(get_modulation_position(note6{int}){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}){Builtin, None} / 127, articulation_volume_curve[instrument_slot2{int}, keyswitch3{int}]{int}){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}){Builtin, None} / 127) * subarticulation_modulation_strength0{real})){Builtin, None}
end function

function articulations_compute_volume_curve(min2 : int, max2 : int, x16 : real, curve0 : int)
	return (int(round(real(min2{int}){Builtin, None} + (real(max2{int} - min2{int}){Builtin, None} * pow(x16{real}, (real(curve0{int}){Builtin, None} / 100) + 1){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function articulations_compute_modulation(instrument_slot3 : int, keyswitch4 : int, note7 : int, subarticulation3 : int, base1 : real)
	return (int((base1{real} * (real(loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[instrument_slot3{int}, keyswitch4{int}, subarticulation3{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} + ((real(get_modulation_position(note7{int}){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}){Builtin, None} / 127) * real(loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_upper[instrument_slot3{int}, keyswitch4{int}, subarticulation3{int}]{int} - loaded_subarticulations_dynamic_range_lower[instrument_slot3{int}, keyswitch4{int}, subarticulation3{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}))) / 127){Builtin, None})
end function

function humanize_by_ms(time0 : int)
	return (random(- time0{int} / 2, time0{int} / 2){Builtin, None})
end function

function is_in_note_selection
	result0{int} := FALSE{int}
	select(note_selection0{int})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_OFF{int}
		result0{int} := TRUE{int}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_LOWEST{int}
		result0{int} := eq(idx16{int}, 0){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_LOWEST_TWO{int}
		result0{int} := eq(idx16{int}, 0){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} + eq(idx16{int}, 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_LOWEST_AND_LOWER_MIDDLE{int}
		result0{int} := (eq(idx16{int}, 0){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} + (eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} / 2){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * le(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})) + (eq(idx16{int}, (num_pressed_notes0{int} / 2) - 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * gt(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_LOWEST_AND_UPPER_MIDDLE{int}
		result0{int} := (eq(idx16{int}, 0){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} + (eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} / 2){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * le(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})) + (eq(idx16{int}, ((num_pressed_notes0{int} - 1) / 2) + 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * gt(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_MIDDLE{int}
		result0{int} := eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} / 2){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_MIDDLE_TWO{int}
		result0{int} := (((eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} / 2){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * le(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}) + (eq(idx16{int}, (num_pressed_notes0{int} / 2) - 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * gt(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})) + (eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} + (1 / 2)){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * le(num_pressed_notes0{int} + 1, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})) + (eq(idx16{int}, (((num_pressed_notes0{int} + 1) - 1) / 2) + 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * gt(num_pressed_notes0{int} + 1, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_LOWER_MIDDLE{int}
		result0{int} := (eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} / 2){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * le(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}) + (eq(idx16{int}, (num_pressed_notes0{int} / 2) - 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * gt(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_UPPER_MIDDLE{int}
		result0{int} := (eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} / 2){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * le(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}) + (eq(idx16{int}, ((num_pressed_notes0{int} - 1) / 2) + 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * gt(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_HIGHEST{int}
		result0{int} := eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} - 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_HIGHEST_TWO{int}
		result0{int} := eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} - 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} + eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} - 2){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_HIGHEST_AND_LOWER_MIDDLE{int}
		result0{int} := (eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} - 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} + (eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} / 2){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * le(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})) + (eq(idx16{int}, (num_pressed_notes0{int} / 2) - 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * gt(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})
	case NOTE_SELECTION_HIGHEST_AND_UPPER_MIDDLE{int}
		result0{int} := (eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} - 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} + (eq(idx16{int}, num_pressed_notes0{int} / 2){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * le(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})) + (eq(idx16{int}, ((num_pressed_notes0{int} - 1) / 2) + 1){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc} * gt(num_pressed_notes0{int}, 3){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc})
	case -2147483648 to 134217727
		result0{int} := 0
	end select
	is_in_note_selection_boolean{int} := bool(result0{int}){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}
end function

function update_selected_notes
	ks2{int} := 0
	pressed_key_idx{int} := 0
	i{int} := 127
	while(i{int} >= 0) 
		if(pressed_keys[i{int}]{int} > (ENGINE_UPTIME{int} - input_acceptance_time{int}))
			inst{int} := 0
			while(inst{int} <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} - 1)) 
						idx16{int} := (num_pressed_keys{int} - 1) - pressed_key_idx{int}
						num_pressed_notes0{int} := num_pressed_keys{int}
						note_selection0{int} := note_selections[inst{int}]{int}
						result0{int} := result00{int}
						call is_in_note_selection{UserDefined, Call}


				if(is_in_note_selection_boolean{int} = TRUE{int})
					pressed_notes_per_instrument[inst{int}, i{int}]{int} := ON{int}
							instrument_slot0{int} := inst{int}
							note4{int} := i{int}
							velocity1{int} := key_velocity[i{int}]{int}
							timing_offset0{int} := pressed_keys[i{int}]{int} - ENGINE_UPTIME{int}
							ks0{int} := result00{int}
							i8{int} := i80{int}
							articulation_event_id5{int} := articulation_event_id50{int}
							set_articulation_event_id0{int} := set_articulation_event_id00{int}
							next_free_idx00{int} := next_free_idx000{int}
							idx180{int} := idx1800{int}
							i40{int} := i400{int}
							is_free00{int} := is_free000{int}
							_ret000{int} := _ret0000{int}
							result100{int} := result1000{int}
							i500{int} := i5000{int}
							reduced_note00{int} := reduced_note000{int}
							string00{int} := string000{int}
							is_free10{int} := is_free100{int}
							_ret1500{int} := _ret15000{int}
							result110{int} := result1100{int}
							call articulations_on_note{UserDefined, Call}


				else
					pressed_notes_per_instrument[inst{int}, i{int}]{int} := OFF{int}
							instrument_slot1{int} := inst{int}
							note5{int} := i{int}
							ks1{int} := result00{int}
							i9{int} := articulation_event_id50{int}
							release_offset0{int} := set_articulation_event_id00{int}
							_ret220{int} := i400{int}
							result20{int} := next_free_idx000{int}
							result21{int} := idx1800{int}
							is_active00{int} := is_free100{int}
							i60{int} := i80{int}
							i501{int} := is_free000{int}
							result22{int} := result1000{int}
							result23{int} := i5000{int}
							result30{int} := reduced_note000{int}
							result24{int} := string000{int}
							call articulations_note_off{UserDefined, Call}


				end if
				inc(inst{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
		else
			if(pressed_keys[i{int}]{int} > 0)
				inst{int} := 0
				while(inst{int} <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} - 1)) 
							idx16{int} := (num_pressed_keys{int} - 1) - pressed_key_idx{int}
							num_pressed_notes0{int} := num_pressed_keys{int}
							note_selection0{int} := note_selections[inst{int}]{int}
							result0{int} := string000{int}
							call is_in_note_selection{UserDefined, Call}


					if(is_in_note_selection_boolean{int} = FALSE{int})
								instrument_slot1{int} := inst{int}
								note5{int} := i{int}
								ks1{int} := string000{int}
								i9{int} := reduced_note000{int}
								release_offset0{int} := i5000{int}
								_ret220{int} := result1000{int}
								result20{int} := is_free000{int}
								result21{int} := i80{int}
								is_active00{int} := is_free100{int}
								i60{int} := idx1800{int}
								i501{int} := next_free_idx000{int}
								result22{int} := i400{int}
								result23{int} := set_articulation_event_id00{int}
								result30{int} := articulation_event_id50{int}
								result24{int} := result00{int}
								call articulations_note_off{UserDefined, Call}


						pressed_notes_per_instrument[inst{int}, i{int}]{int} := OFF{int}
					end if
					inc(inst{int}){Builtin, None}
				end while
			end if
		end if
		if(pressed_keys[i{int}]{int} > 0)
			inc(pressed_key_idx{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		dec(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
	inst{int} := 0
	while(inst{int} <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} - 1)) 
		active_notes[inst{int}]{int} := 0
		i{int} := 0
		while(i{int} <= 127) 
			if(pressed_notes_per_instrument[inst{int}, i{int}]{int} = ON{int})
				inc(active_notes[inst{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if
			inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		inc(inst{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function get_next_rr
	rr1{int} := 0
	if(subarticulations_rrr[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}]{int}]{int}]{int} = 0)
		if(loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}]{int} = 0)
			rr1{int} := (rr_data_idx[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}, note14{int}]{int} + 1) mod subarticulations_rr_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}]{int}]{int}]{int}
		else
			rr1{int} := random(0, subarticulations_rr_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}]{int}]{int}]{int} - 1){Builtin, None}
		end if
	else
		if((ENGINE_UPTIME{int} - rr_data_time[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}, note14{int}]{int}) > subarticulations_rrr_reset_time[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}]{int}]{int}]{int})
			if(loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}]{int} = 0)
				rr1{int} := (rr_data_idx[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}, note14{int}]{int} + 1) mod subarticulations_rrr[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}]{int}]{int}]{int}
			else
				rr1{int} := random(0, subarticulations_rrr[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}]{int}]{int}]{int} - 1){Builtin, None}
			end if
		else
			if(loaded_subarticulations_rr_mode[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}]{int} = 0)
				rr1{int} := max(subarticulations_rrr[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}]{int}]{int}]{int}, (rr_data_idx[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}, note14{int}]{int} + 1) mod subarticulations_rr_num[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument5{int}, keyswitch9{int}, subarticulation_idx3{int}]{int}]{int}]{int}){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}

										transpose00{int} := octave_shift[inst0{int}]{int} * 12
										octave_layer00{int} := octave_layer[inst0{int}]{int}
										previous_note00{int} := repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[_iter40{int}]{int}
										subarticulation_event_id180{int} := rr11{int}
										idx2201{int} := idx2200{int}
										result601{int} := result600{int}
										transition_note_event02{int} := transition_note_event01{int}
										transition_octave_event02{int} := transition_octave_event01{int}
										i152{int} := i151{int}
										ii22{int} := ii21{int}
										idx2302{int} := idx2301{int}
										end_note22{int} := end_note21{int}
										transition_note02{int} := transition_note01{int}
										transition_type22{int} := transition_type21{int}
										transition_dyn_layer02{int} := transition_dyn_layer01{int}
										offset12{int} := offset11{int}
										transition_speed01{real} := transition_speed00{real}
										_ret4002{int} := _ret4001{int}
										result702{int} := result701{int}
										i1202{int} := i1201{int}
										i11002{int} := i11001{int}
										i1302{int} := i1301{int}
										event102{int} := event101{int}
										octave_event002{int} := octave_event001{int}
										i1402{int} := i1401{int}
										ii102{int} := ii101{int}
										_ret57002{int} := _ret57001{int}
										reduced_note0102{int} := reduced_note0101{int}
										string0102{int} := string0101{int}
										string0202{int} := string0201{int}
										call subarticulation_play_note0{UserDefined, Call}



									articulation_event_id11{int} := subarticulation_event_articulation_event[repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[_iter40{int}]{int}]{int}
									subarticulation11{int} := subarticulation_event_subarticulation_idx[repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[_iter40{int}]{int}]{int}
									subarticulation_event_id171{int} := id0{int}
									call articulation_event_set_subarticulation_event_id1{UserDefined, Call}


							subarticulation_event_articulation_event[id0{int}]{int} := subarticulation_event_articulation_event[repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[_iter40{int}]{int}]{int}
							rr11{int} := repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[_iter40{int}]{int}
									subarticulation_event1{int} := rr11{int}
									idx25{int} := result701{int}
									call repetition_engine_remove{UserDefined, Call}


						end if
					else
						inst0{int} := repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[_iter40{int}]{int}
								subarticulation_event1{int} := inst0{int}
								idx25{int} := timing0{int}
								call repetition_engine_remove{UserDefined, Call}


					end if
				end if
				inc(_iter40{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while

		if(any_event_played0{int} = TRUE{int})
					new_tempo0{real} := transition_speed00{real}
					i0{int} := _iter40{int}
					ii0{int} := inst0{int}
					iii0{int} := timing0{int}
					call repetition_engine_update_tempo{UserDefined, Call}


			i{int} := 0
			while((i{int} < num_elements[repetition_played_subarticulation_events{int[]}]) and (repetition_played_subarticulation_events[i{int}]{int} # - 1)) 
				repetition_interval_time_humanization[articulation_event_instrument[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[repetition_played_subarticulation_events[i{int}]{int}]{int}]{int}, articulation_event_keyswitch[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[repetition_played_subarticulation_events[i{int}]{int}]{int}]{int}, subarticulation_event_subarticulation_idx[repetition_played_subarticulation_events[i{int}]{int}]{int}]{int} := humanize_by_ms(articulation_humanization[articulation_event_instrument[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[repetition_played_subarticulation_events[i{int}]{int}]{int}]{int}, articulation_event_keyswitch[subarticulation_event_articulation_event[repetition_played_subarticulation_events[i{int}]{int}]{int}]{int}]{int}){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}
				inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
		end if
		if(any_event_active0{int} = FALSE{int})
			repetition_engine_active{int} := FALSE{int}
			repetition_engine_start_time{int} := - 1
		end if
	end if
end function

function repetition_engine_update_tempo
	new_tempo0{real} := real(ms_to_ticks(60000000){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} / 960
	if((new_tempo0{real} # tempo{real}) or (NI_CALLBACK_TYPE{int} # NI_CB_TYPE_LISTENER{int}))
		i0{int} := 0
		ii0{int} := 0
		iii0{int} := 0
		i0{int} := 0
		while(i0{int} <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} - 1)) 
			ii0{int} := 0
			while(ii0{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
				iii0{int} := 0
				while(iii0{int} <= (NUM_SUBARTICULATIONS{int} - 1)) 
					if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[i0{int}, ii0{int}, iii0{int}]{int}]{int}]{int} = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_REPETITION{int})
						repetition_interval_time[i0{int}, ii0{int}, iii0{int}]{int} := int((60000 / new_tempo0{real}) * (4 / real(loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[i0{int}, ii0{int}, iii0{int}]{int}){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}
					end if
					inc(iii0{int}){Builtin, None}
				end while
				inc(ii0{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
			inc(i0{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		tempo{real} := new_tempo0{real}
	end if
end function

function repetition_engine_add
	idx23{int} := search[repetition_engine_subarticulation_events{int[]}, - 1]
	if(idx23{int} # - 1)
		repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[idx23{int}]{int} := subarticulation_event0{int}
		repetition_engine_active{int} := TRUE{int}
		if(repetition_engine_start_time{int} = - 1)
			repetition_engine_start_time{int} := ENGINE_UPTIME{int}
		end if
	else
		message("REACHED MAX_SUBARTICULATIONS_IN_REPETITION_ENGINE"){Builtin, None}
	end if
end function

function repetition_engine_remove
	idx25{int} := search[repetition_engine_subarticulation_events{int[]}, subarticulation_event1{int}]
	if(idx25{int} # - 1)
		repetition_engine_subarticulation_events[idx25{int}]{int} := - 1
	end if
end function

end function

end function

function set_key_colors
	i3{int} := 0
	i3{int} := 0
	while(i3{int} <= 127) 
		set_key_color(i3{int}, KEY_COLOR_WHITE{int}){Builtin, None}
		if((i3{int} >= 55) and (i3{int} <= 96))
			set_key_color(i3{int}, KEY_COLOR_BLUE{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i3{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function update_keyswitch_volume_curve

	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (num_elements[lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{int[]}] - 1)) 
		set_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT{int}, articulations_compute_volume_curve(int((real(articulation_volume_min[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None}, int((real(articulation_volume_max[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None}, real(i{int}){Builtin, None} / real(num_elements[lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{int[]}]){Builtin, None}, articulation_volume_curve[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}]{int}){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}){Builtin, None}

end function

function update_modwheel_assignment_circles
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (4 - 1)) 
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, i{int}]{int} # - 1)
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
			if(i{int} = selected_subarticulation{int})
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-selected-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-handle-left-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-handle-right-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
			else
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-unselected-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-darken-left-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
				set_control_par_str(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int}, "modwheel-circle-darken-right-" & i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end if
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_left[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, i{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
			set_control_par(lbl_center_circle_bound_right[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int}, 127 - loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, i{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

			modwheel3{int} := get_modulation_position(0){UserDefined, ExpressionFunc}

function editor_update_modwheel_position
			modwheel3{int} := modwheel4{int}
			call update_dynamic_range_cursor{UserDefined, Call}


			modwheel2{int} := modwheel4{int}
			call update_circle_modwheel_position{UserDefined, Call}


			modwheel1{int} := modwheel4{int}
			call update_modwheel_assignment_cursor{UserDefined, Call}


			modwheel0{int} := modwheel4{int}
			call update_keyswitch_volume_curve_cursor{UserDefined, Call}


end function

function center_circle_distance
	dx0{real} := x17{real} - 0.5
	dy0{real} := y3{real} - 0.5
	ret15{real} := sqrt((dx0{real} * dx0{real}) + (dy0{real} * dy0{real})){Builtin, None}
end function

function center_circle_angle
	dx1{real} := x18{real} - 0.5
	dy1{real} := y4{real} - 0.5
	cos_theta0{real} := dx1{real} / sqrt((dx1{real} * dx1{real}) + (dy1{real} * dy1{real})){Builtin, None}
	angle1{real} := acos(cos_theta0{real}){Builtin, None}
	if(dy1{real} < 0)
		angle1{real} := (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real}) - angle1{real}
	end if
	ret16{real} := angle1{real}
end function

function angle_to_value
	new_angle0{real} := angle0{real} + (NI_MATH_PI{real} / 2)
	if(new_angle0{real} > (NI_MATH_PI{real} * 2))
		new_angle0{real} := new_angle0{real} - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real})
	end if
	new_angle0{real} := abs(new_angle0{real} - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real})){Builtin, None}
	ret17{int} := int((127 * (new_angle0{real} - angle_min0{real})) / (angle_max0{real} - angle_min0{real})){Builtin, None}
end function

				i17{int} := i170{int}

function swi_keyswitch_ui_controls{restricted}
	idx26{int} := search[swi_keyswitch{int[]}, uiid1{int}]
	if(idx26{int} # - 1)
		if(get_control_par(swi_keyswitch[idx26{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_KEY_SHIFT{int}){Builtin, None} = OFF{int})
			i{int} := 0
			while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
				keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int}, i{int}]{int} := OFF{int}
				inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
			end while
		end if
		keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int}, idx26{int}]{int} := ON{int}
		selected_keyswitch{int} := idx26{int}
				idx17000{int} := idx170001{int}
				call update_keyswitch_selection{UserDefined, Call}


	end if
	idx26{int} := search[swi_keyswitch_purge{int[]}, uiid1{int}]
	if(idx26{int} # - 1)
		keyswitch_purge_states[selected_instrument{int}, idx26{int}]{int} := get_control_par(swi_keyswitch_purge[idx26{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}){Builtin, None}
				i17{int} := idx170001{int}
				ii4{int} := ii40{int}
				iii1{int} := iii10{int}
				_ret6600{int} := _ret66000{int}
				group_count000{int} := group_count0000{int}
				group_count001{int} := group_count0010{int}
				update_purge{UserDefined, Inlining}


	end if
end function

function update_keyswitch_selection
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
		set_control_par(swi_keyswitch[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int}, i{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par_str(lbl_keyswitch[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int}, "          "){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par_str(lbl_keyswitch[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXTLINE{int}, "          "){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par_str(lbl_keyswitch[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXTLINE{int}, articulation_names[selected_instrument{int}, i{int}]{string}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(swi_keyswitch_purge[i{int}]{int}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int}, keyswitch_purge_states[selected_instrument{int}, i{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
		set_key_pressed((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int}, i{int}]{int}){Builtin, None}
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
		keyswitches_color_keys{UserDefined, Inlining}

	selected_subarticulation{int} := 0
	if(get_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_editor_page{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}){Builtin, None} = HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int})
				idx1700{int} := idx17000{int}
				editor_page_open{UserDefined, Inlining}


		if(get_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_subarticulation_browser{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}){Builtin, None} = HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int})
					i20{int} := idx17000{int}
					subarticulation_browser_open{UserDefined, Inlining}


		end if
	end if
end function

function keyswitches_color_keys
	i{int} := 0
	while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
		set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, KEY_COLOR_RED{int}){Builtin, None}
		if(keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int}, i{int}]{int} = ON{int})
			set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}, KEY_COLOR_ORANGE{int}){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function keyswitches_on_note
	check_before0{int} := 0
	changed0{int} := FALSE{int}
	if(in_range(note16{int}, keyswitch_octave{int} * 12, ((keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int}) - 1){Builtin, None})
		i{int} := 0
		while(i{int} <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} - 1)) 
			check_before0{int} := keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int}, i{int}]{int}
			keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int}, i{int}]{int} := KEY_DOWN[(keyswitch_octave{int} * 12) + i{int}]{int}
			if(check_before0{int} # keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int}, i{int}]{int})
				changed0{int} := TRUE{int}
			end if
			selected_keyswitch{int} := note16{int} - (keyswitch_octave{int} * 12)
			inc(i{int}){Builtin, None}
		end while
		if(changed0{int} = TRUE{int})
					idx17000{int} := idx170000{int}
					call update_keyswitch_selection{UserDefined, Call}


		end if
	end if
end function

function subarticulation_browser_open
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_subarticulation_browser{int}){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int}, HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int}){Builtin, None}
	if(loaded_subarticulations[selected_instrument{int}, selected_keyswitch{int}, selected_subarticulation{int}]{int} # - 1)

function transition_notes_to_type(start_note1 : int, end_note1 : int)

end function
